Ancestors of VROMEN, Vincentius Magdalena Franciscus (Vincent)

 

GENERATION I

 
1  VROMEN, Vincentius Magdalena Franciscus (Vincent)
Son of Antonius Marcellinus Maria Gerardus (Antoine) Vromen (see 2) and Maria Elisabeth (Liesbeth) Herings (see 3).
 

GENERATION II

 
2  VROMEN, Antonius Marcellinus Maria Gerardus (Antoine); son of Jan Joseph (Jeun) Vromen (see 4) and Caecilia Wilhelmina Jozefina (Cecile) Overhof (see 5).
He had a relationship with
3  HERINGS, Maria Elisabeth (Liesbeth); daughter of Jan Joseph Herings (see 6) and Maria Katharina (Kate) Wienands (see 7).
From this relation:                         VROMEN, Vincentius Magdalena Franciscus (Vincent)  [1]
 

GENERATION III

 
4  VROMEN, Jan Joseph (Jeun); he was born 8 July 1927 at Brunssum (NL/LI), Gas-technician, died 7 December 1980 id., son of Antoon Joseph Vromen (see 8) and Maria Helena Bex (see 9).
He married 19 January 1960 at Brunssum (NL/LI)
5  OVERHOF, Caecilia Wilhelmina Jozefina (Cecile); she was born 16 April 1924 at Kerkrade (NL/LI), Shop-assistant Jamin, died 18 December 1998 at Heerlen (NL/LI), buried at Brunssum (NL/LI), daughter of Hubertus Johannes Overhof (see 10) and Maria Hubertina Cap (see 11).
From this marriage:                         VROMEN, Antonius Marcellinus Maria Gerardus (Antoine)  [2]
 
6  HERINGS, Jan Joseph; son of Arnold Joseph Herings (see 12) and Maria Anna Beumers (see 13).
He had a relationship with
7  WIENANDS, Maria Katharina (Kate); she was born 6 February 1927 at Stahe Gangelt (D), died 3 January 2005 at Heerlen (NL/LI), buried at Schinveld (NL/LI), daughter of Franz Josef Wienands (see 14) and Anna Barbara Meeszen (see 15).
From this relation:                         HERINGS, Maria Elisabeth (Liesbeth)  [3]
 

GENERATION IV

 
8  VROMEN, Antoon Joseph; he was born 13 March 1892 at Brunssum (NL/LI), Merchant, died 10 September 1963 id., son of Willem Joseph Vromen (see 16) and Virginia Mechtildis VAN Eeghem (see 17).
He married 18 May 1921 at Brunssum (NL/LI)
9  BEX, Maria Helena; she was born 26 May 1895 at Brunssum (NL/LI), died 26 March 1979 id., daughter of Peter Joseph Bex (see 18) and Maria Catharina DRESSCHERS Dreschers (see 19).
From this marriage:        8-7-1927  -  7-12-1980 VROMEN, Jan Joseph (Jeun)  [4]
 
10  OVERHOF, Hubertus Johannes; he was born 24 May 1883 at Maastricht (NL/LI), died 10 November 1939 at Brunssum (NL/LI), son of Petrus Overhof (see 20) and Maria Anna Clairbois (see 21).
He married 17 May 1905 at Maastricht (NL/LI)
11  CAP, Maria Hubertina; she was born 29 July 1880 at Maastricht (NL/LI), died 9 March 1960 at Brunssum (NL/LI), daughter of Franciscus Cap (see 22) and Wilhelmina Leseur (see 23).
From this marriage:        16-4-1924  -  18-12-1998 OVERHOF, Caecilia Wilhelmina Jozefina (Cecile)  [5]
 
12  HERINGS, Arnold Joseph; he was born 25 November 1889 at Schinveld (NL/LI), Blacksmith/Farmer, died 30 October 1969 id., son of Peter Mathias Herings (see 24) and Maria Catharina or Maria Josephina or Anna Josephina Dassen (see 25).
He married 20 June 1919 at Schinveld (NL/LI)
13  BEUMERS, Maria Anna; she was born 14 May 1891 at Waldhauserhohe (bij Monchen-Gladbach) (D), died 14 August 1968 at Brunssum (NL/LI), daughter of Jan Felix Beumers (see 26) and Maria Catharina Hubertina Daemen (see 27).
From this marriage:                         HERINGS, Jan Joseph  [6]
 
14  WIENANDS, Franz Josef; he was born 17 May 1878 at Stahe (D), municipal labourer, died 11 February 1946 id., son of Egidius Wienands (see 28) and Josefina of Mechtilde Dassen (see 29).
